 ) a new mental health app is designed to help people recover from earthquake shock and promote their general well-being
 samachar patr 'da press' ke mutabik, is nae ap ko newjiland ke ek saarvajanik swasthya abhiyaan 'ol rhite?' dwaara taiyaar kiya gaya he, jiskaa uddeshy bukamp ke bhaavnaatmak prabhaavon se logon ko ubaarana he
 App users will be provided easy 'mini missions' daily to improve mental health
 in mini mishnon ko puraa karne ke baad ap unhen sakaaratmak pratikriya ke saath inaam degaa
 'all right?' Key public health expert Lucy Deith said, "there is a lot of evidence that the right care and thinking in times of stress energize daily life
" haalanki achche maansik swasthya or behatari ke liye koi jaadu kii chadi nahin he
 "comments is ap main shaamil mishan 'acchhee tarah se rahane ke paanch tareekon' se sambandhit hai, jise england ke new iconomics foundation ne dizin kiya he
 These include connecting with others, learning new things, giving time to others and focusing on the good things around them
 yah ap, appal ap store or android phone ke liye google play par uplabdh he
 According to the newspaper 'the Press', this new app was called 'all Right?', a New Zealand public health campaign
 Prepared by, which aims to rescue people from the emotional effects of earthquakes
 ap upyogkartaaon ko maansik swasthya sudhaarney ke liye pratidin aasaan 'mini mishan' uplabdh karaae jaaenge
 After completing these mini missions the app will reward them with positive feedback
 'ol rhite?' kii saarvajanik swasthya visheshgy lusi dith ne kaha, "aise kai pramaan hai, jinase pataa chalata he ki tanaav ke samay sahi dekharekh or soch se dainik jivan main sphurti aati he
 However there is no magic wand for good mental health and well-being
 "tippaniyan The missions included in this app relate to the 'five ways to live well', designed by the New Economics Foundation of England

 hamaara drushtikon kya he

 i think that as soon as the truth is deeply ingrained in our consciousness that 'I am also a normal part of nature', in the same way, the consciousness of understanding itself disappears, the ego is destroyed and before the eyes All the webs that are made are cleared, which were hindering the seeing of any object clearly
 tippaniyan By the way, if we pay even a little attention, there will be no mistake in catching this deep truth of life that at the root of most of our problems and crises, this manure called 'ego' is doing its job

 bataa den ki baleen whales ko prithvi par sabase bada jaanavar mana jaataa he

 iske liye wo khaas takanic kaa sahaara le rahe hai

 but it is a different voice '

 The Border Security Force (BSF) spotted the drone on Monday night at Hussainiwala on the india-pakistan border
 iske baad biguef javaanon ne drone par firing kii
 The drone moved back to Pakistan due to firing
 iske baad biguef ne search oparation chalaaya
 Also, every activity is being monitored along the border
 bataa den isse 16 oktober ko pehle punjab ke ferozepur main ek baar phir pakistani drone dekha gaya tha
 Villagers of Hazara Singh Wala and Bakri, a border village on the international border, saw the drone flying
 sthaneey logon kaa kahana he ki drone bhartiya kshetra main ek kilometre tak ghusaa tha

 biguef ke echke tower ke paas bahut oonchi udaan bhar rahaa tha
 However, no information has been received regarding whether the drone had dropped anything
 ise satluj nadi ke kinare dhan ke kheton par bhi dekha gaya tha
 However, it is not clear whether BSF personnel were successful in killing the drone
 pakistan or china ke saath simaaon par badhate khataron se paar paane ke liye bhartiya sena aise drone kharidne kii yojana bana rahi he, jo saamaan kii dhulaai karne or missile kii tarah atake karne main sakasham honge

 The Parliament today approved the bill providing maximum death penalty to the culprits of damaging petroleum products pipelines in the country
 aatankwaadi krityon ke liye nunatam das saal kii sajaa ke praavdhaan vaale petroleum or khanij pipeline (bhoomi ke upyog ke adhikaar kaa arjan) vidheyak ko buudhvaar ko rajyasabha kii dhvanimat se manjuuri mil gayi
 The Lok Sabha has already passed it
 ucch sadan main vidheyak par hui charchaa kaa jawaab dete hue petroleum evam prakritik gas rajyamantri arpyen singh ne aashwaasan diya ki sarkaar desh main tel evam gas pipelinon kii suraksha vyavastha ko pukhta banane ke is kaam main un kisaanon or logon ko shaamil karne ke suzav par gambhirtha se vichaar karegi jinaki bhoomi se pipeline guzarati he
 He said that rights will also be considered for Gram Panchayats for this purpose
 vidheyak main aropiyon par khud ko nirdosh sabit karne kaa jimmaa daale jane par kuch sadasyon dwaara aapatti jataaye jane par mantri ne kaha ki yah praavdhaan ke keval mafia or todphod karne waalon par lagu hoga unhone kaha ki dand ke bataur maut kii sajaa kaa praavdhaan bahut hi kam maamalon ke liye he
 He said that the first offense of tampering with a pipeline will carry a sentence of six months, but the amount of punishment will be increased for such a mistake again
 singh ne spasht kiya ki aatankwaadi yaa naksalwadi girohon dwaara aisi vaardaat ko anjaam dene kii sthiti main unke liye mrityudand kaa praavdhaan kiya gaya he
 He made it clear that the government will try not to take such action against innocent people
 assam main aatankwaadi ghatnaon se pipelinon kii todphod ke bare main sadasyon kii dharna ke sandarbh main unhone kaha ki ascharyajanak rup se zyada risaav tathaa durupyog ke sabase zyada maamle rajasthan or haryana main dekhne ko mili hai
 The Minister of State for Petroleum said that 18,900 km of new pipelines will be laid in the 12th Five Year Plan
